= Coffee Fleet OTA + Cloud Design
:toc:
:toclevels: 2
:sectnums:

== Introduction

This document models connected coffee machines that send <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_TELEMETRY,telemetry>> to a <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_CENTRAL_CLOUD_SITE,central cloud site>>,
receive OTA firmware updates, and produce operational and audit logging <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_EVIDENCE,evidence>>.
Authored functional architecture remains stable while runtime, code, and verification layers
are inferred from infrastructure, source, and test artifacts.

=== Scope and Assumptions

- <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_EM_FUNCTIONAL_GROUP,Functional Groups>> and <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_EM_FUNCTIONAL_UNIT,Functional Units>> are the stable authored design backbone.
- <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_EM_RUNTIME_ELEMENT,Runtime elements>> and <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_EM_CODE_ELEMENT,code elements>> are inferred from available IaC, deployment, and source artifacts.
- Inferred coverage is evidence-driven and may be partial when source metadata is missing.
- <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_EM_REQUIREMENT,Requirements>> and reference indexes are provided for traceability, not as primary narrative flow.

== How To Read This Document

This document is intentionally split into two layers:

1. Concept layer: functional and view-specific architecture narratives for human understanding.
2. Evidence layer: generated requirement traceability and inferred reference indexes.

Read in this order:

1. Architecture Intent View: stable authored architecture intent and ownership boundaries.
2. Communication / Deployment / Security Views: viewpoint-specific operational behavior.
3. Traceability View: requirement mapping, evidence coverage, and confidence.
4. Reference Appendix: supporting reference IDs and inferred-source links.

++++

|===

|An authored lifecycle state used to model transition behavior, guards, and event-driven progression.
|[[REF_ENGMODEL_TERM_STRUCTURIZR_DSL]]<<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_STRUCTURIZR_DSL,Structurizr DSL>> (TERM-STRUCTURIZR-DSL)
|Generated Structurizr DSL workspace that projects authored architecture, relationships, dynamic views, and deployment metadata.
|[[REF_CATALOG_EVT_TELEMETRY_INGESTED]]<<REF_IDX-CATALOG_EVT_TELEMETRY_INGESTED,telemetry ingested event is received>> (EVT-TELEMETRY-INGESTED)
|Event raised when cloud ingestion accepts telemetry. Aliases:fleet events, ingestion events, observability event fanout, observability events, telemetry ingested
|[[REF_CATALOG_AV_TELEMETRY_REPLAY_ABUSE]]<<REF_IDX-CATALOG_AV_TELEMETRY_REPLAY_ABUSE,telemetry replay abuse>> (AV-TELEMETRY-REPLAY-ABUSE)
|Replayed telemetry floods ingestion and distorts reporting. Aliases:telemetry replay
|[[REF_CATALOG_EVT_TELEMETRY_REPLAY_ABUSE_DETECTED]]<<REF_IDX-CATALOG_EVT_TELEMETRY_REPLAY_ABUSE_DETECTED,telemetry replay abuse is detected>> (EVT-TELEMETRY-REPLAY-ABUSE-DETECTED)
|Event raised when replayed telemetry behavior is detected and flagged as abuse. Aliases:replay abuse, telemetry replay detected
|[[REF_ENGMODEL_TERM_THREAT_ASSUMPTION]]<<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_THREAT_ASSUMPTION,threat assumption>> (TERM-THREAT-ASSUMPTION)
|Authored security assumption that records scope, rationale, owner, status, and evidence.
|[[REF_ENGMODEL_TERM_THREAT_DRAGON_DOCUMENT]]<<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_THREAT_DRAGON_DOCUMENT,Threat Dragon document>> (TERM-THREAT-DRAGON-DOCUMENT)
|Threat Dragon JSON representation generated from the engineering model for STRIDE threat-model review.
|[[REF_ENGMODEL_TERM_THREAT_MITIGATION]]<<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_THREAT_MITIGATION,threat mitigation>> (TERM-THREAT-MITIGATION)
|Authored mitigation record that links a threat scenario to a control, effectiveness, verification, and evidence.
|[[REF_ENGMODEL_TERM_THREAT_MODEL_EXPORT]]<<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_THREAT_MODEL_EXPORT,threat model export>> (TERM-THREAT-MODEL-EXPORT)
|Generated security artifact that translates authored architecture, flows, trust boundaries, threats, and mitigations into an external threat-model schema.
|[[REF_ENGMODEL_TERM_THREAT_OUT_OF_SCOPE]]<<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_THREAT_OUT_OF_SCOPE,threat out-of-scope decision>> (TERM-THREAT-OUT-OF-SCOPE)
|Authored decision that excludes a threat concern from current scope with reason, owner, expiry, and evidence.
|[[REF_ENGMODEL_TERM_THREAT_SCENARIO]]<<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_THREAT_SCENARIO,threat scenario>> (TERM-THREAT-SCENARIO)
|Authored threat narrative that connects attack vectors, scope, flows, controls, risks, and verification evidence.
|[[REF_ENGMODEL_TERM_TRACE_MARKER]]<<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_TRACE_MARKER,trace marker>> (TERM-TRACE-MARKER)
|Source-level marker such as TRLC-LINKS or ENGMODEL-LINKS used to connect declarations to requirements and model entities.
|[[REF_ENGMODEL_TERM_TRLC_PACKAGE]]<<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_TRLC_PACKAGE,TRLC package>> (TERM-TRLC-PACKAGE)
|Generated TRLC model and requirements package used for formal requirement traceability processing.
|[[REF_ENGMODEL_TERM_TRUST_BOUNDARY]]<<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_TRUST_BOUNDARY,trust boundary>> (TERM-TRUST-BOUNDARY)
|An authored trust separation zone that marks policy, identity, or security control boundaries.
|[[REF_CATALOG_FU_UPDATE_CAMPAIGN_ORCHESTRATION]]<<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_UPDATE_CAMPAIGN_ORCHESTRATION,update campaign orchestration>> (FU-UPDATE-CAMPAIGN-ORCHESTRATION)
|Selects target machine groups and coordinates OTA rollout phases. Aliases:campaign orchestration
|[[REF_ENGMODEL_TERM_UPWARD_LINKING]]<<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_UPWARD_LINKING,upward linking>> (TERM-UPWARD-LINKING)
|Rule where runtime and code elements point to stable functional groups/units; authored architecture does not depend on inferred IDs.
|[[REF_ENGMODEL_TERM_VALIDATION]]<<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_VALIDATION,validation>> (TERM-VALIDATION)
|Model quality gate that checks authored documents, references, relationship semantics, and requirement lint results.
|[[REF_ENGMODEL_TERM_VALIDATION_DIAGNOSTIC]]<<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_VALIDATION_DIAGNOSTIC,validation diagnostic>> (TERM-VALIDATION-DIAGNOSTIC)
|Structured validation finding with code, severity, message, and optional source path.
|[[REF_ENGMODEL_TERM_VERIFICATION_CHECK]]<<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_VERIFICATION_CHECK,verification check>> (TERM-VERIFICATION-CHECK)
|An inferred or authored verification artifact that validates requirement behavior with test evidence.
|[[REF_ENGMODEL_TERM_VIEW]]<<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_VIEW,view>> (TERM-VIEW)
|Authored projection configuration that selects roots, entity kinds, mappings, audience, and abstraction.
|===

== Architecture Intent View

Show the stable authored architecture intent: capability areas, unit ownership boundaries, and intentional responsibility split.

=== What This View Answers


- What are the main capability areas?

- What are the stable units of responsibility and what does each unit own?

- How are responsibilities intentionally split?

=== Functional Groups and Units (View Scoped)



==== Machine Edge (FG-MACHINE-EDGE)


Device-local <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_TELEMETRY,telemetry>> and OTA execution responsibilities.

	

	<<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FG_MACHINE_EDGE,Machine Edge>> owns behavior that executes directly on coffee machines.
It gathers <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_TELEMETRY,telemetry>>, applies OTA updates, and reports local status to cloud boundaries.
	

	
===== Functional Unit Dependency Diagram

What this diagram shows: dependencies involving functional units in this functional group. Units in this group are rendered inside the group container; connected external units and referenced elements are shown outside it.

[source,mermaid]
----
flowchart LR
  subgraph FGDEP_FG_MACHINE_EDGE["Machine Edge"]
    direction TB
    FU_FU_MACHINE_TELEMETRY_COLLECTION["Machine Telemetry Collection"]:::functional_unit
    FU_FU_OTA_UPDATE_AGENT["OTA Update Agent"]:::functional_unit
    subgraph RT_FU_MACHINE_TELEMETRY_COLLECTION_MACHINE_TELEMETRY_COLLECTION_RUNTIME__INFERRED_["Machine Telemetry Collection runtime (inferred)"]
      direction TB
      CODE_MACHINE_TELEMETRY_RS["machine_telemetry.rs"]:::code_element
    end

===== Machine Telemetry Collection (FU-MACHINE-TELEMETRY-COLLECTION)





Collects brew/device <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_TELEMETRY,telemetry>> and transmits cloud-bound <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_TELEMETRY_PAYLOADS,telemetry payloads>>.

[discrete]
====== Owned Responsibility

functional responsibility for <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_MACHINE_TELEMETRY_COLLECTION,machine telemetry collection>>; includes decision and orchestration <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_FLOW,flow>> to <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_DEVICE_IDENTITY_SECRETS,Device Identity and Secrets>> and decision and orchestration <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_FLOW,flow>> to <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_FLEET_INGESTION_API,Fleet Ingestion API>>

[discrete]
====== Key Collaborators

<<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_DEVICE_IDENTITY_SECRETS,Device Identity and Secrets>>, <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_FLEET_INGESTION_API,Fleet Ingestion API>>, <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_REF_IOT_INGEST_ENDPOINT,IoT Ingest Endpoint>>, <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_REF_MQTT_DEVICE_SDK,MQTT Device SDK>>

[discrete]
====== Linked Requirements

<<REF_IDX-REQ_REQ_COF_001,REQ-COF-001>>, <<REF_IDX-REQ_REQ_COF_006,REQ-COF-006>>, <<REF_IDX-REQ_REQ_COF_011,REQ-COF-011>>






===== OTA Update Agent (FU-OTA-UPDATE-AGENT)





Downloads <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_SIGNED_FIRMWARE_BUNDLES,signed firmware bundles>>, validates integrity, applies updates, and reports status.

[discrete]
====== Owned Responsibility

functional responsibility for <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_OTA_UPDATE_AGENT,ota update agent>>; includes decision and orchestration <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_FLOW,flow>> to <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_DEVICE_IDENTITY_SECRETS,Device Identity and Secrets>> and decision and orchestration <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_FLOW,flow>> to <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_REF_FIRMWARE_BUNDLE_STORE,Firmware Bundle Store>>

[discrete]
====== Key Collaborators

<<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_DEVICE_IDENTITY_SECRETS,Device Identity and Secrets>>, <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_REF_FIRMWARE_BUNDLE_STORE,Firmware Bundle Store>>, <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_UPDATE_CAMPAIGN_ORCHESTRATION,Update Campaign Orchestration>>

[discrete]

<<REF_IDX-REQ_REQ_COF_003,REQ-COF-003>>, <<REF_IDX-REQ_REQ_COF_004,REQ-COF-004>>, <<REF_IDX-REQ_REQ_COF_005,REQ-COF-005>>, <<REF_IDX-REQ_REQ_COF_010,REQ-COF-010>>










==== Cloud Control (FG-CLOUD-CONTROL)


Central cloud ingestion, campaign <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_CONTROL,control>>, and fleet reporting.

	

	<<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FG_CLOUD_CONTROL,Cloud Control>> owns central APIs and coordination logic for fleet <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_TELEMETRY,telemetry>> and <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_OTA_ROLLOUT,OTA rollouts>>.
It provides global fleet visibility and deterministic rollout decisions.

===== Fleet Ingestion API (FU-FLEET-INGESTION-API)





Receives <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_TELEMETRY,telemetry>> and <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_MACHINE_STATUS,machine status>>, applies <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_VALIDATION,validation>>, and emits <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_INGESTION_EVENTS,ingestion events>>.

[discrete]
====== Owned Responsibility

functional responsibility for <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_FLEET_INGESTION_API,fleet ingestion api>>; includes decision and orchestration <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_FLOW,flow>> to <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_REF_CLOUD_RUNTIME_SDK,Cloud Runtime SDK>> and decision and orchestration <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_FLOW,flow>> to <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_DEVICE_IDENTITY_SECRETS,Device Identity and Secrets>>

[discrete]

<<REF_IDX-CATALOG_REF_CLOUD_RUNTIME_SDK,Cloud Runtime SDK>>, <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_DEVICE_IDENTITY_SECRETS,Device Identity and Secrets>>, <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_FLEET_OBSERVABILITY_REPORTING,Fleet Observability Reporting>>

===== Fleet Observability Reporting (FU-FLEET-OBSERVABILITY-REPORTING)

===== Update Campaign Orchestration (FU-UPDATE-CAMPAIGN-ORCHESTRATION)





Plans OTA <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_ROLLOUT_COHORTS,rollout cohorts>>, drives update commands, and handles rollback <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_FLOW,flow>> decisions.

==== Platform Operations (FG-PLATFORM-OPERATIONS)

It ensures cloud and device <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_TRUST_BOUNDARY,trust boundaries>> remain enforceable over time.

== Security View

Show inferred exposure and dependency <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_RISK,risk>> points aligned to unit boundaries, focused on attack paths and security <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_EVIDENCE,evidence>>.

=== What This View Answers


- What are the main <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_TRUST_BOUNDARY,trust boundaries>> and attack paths?

- Which units are exposed and what security <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_EVIDENCE,evidence>> exists?

- Where is the threat <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_MODEL,model>> incomplete?

=== Coverage Gaps

Coverage summary: 6/7 units have direct <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_EVIDENCE,evidence>> coverage in this <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_VIEW,view>>.


- <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_CLOUD_RUNTIME_OPERATIONS,Cloud Runtime Operations>> has no explicit authored attack-vector mapping yet; document technical and fraud/abuse threats even when mitigated.


=== Recommended Next Evidence Additions


- Add explicit authored attack-vector mappings for units currently marked without threat linkage.

- Add security signal ownership metadata (logs/alerts/<<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_EVENT,events>>) for unresolved observability <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_EVIDENCE,evidence>>.

- Map additional security-relevant dependencies and exposures into <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_AUTHORED_MAPPING,authored mappings>> for traceable coverage.

Adversary attempts to alter or suppress security-relevant logs to hide malicious behavior.

|Impact |high
|Severity |medium
|Risk |RISK-COFFEE-LOG-TAMPERING

=== Security Flow Semantics

[cols="1,2,1,1,1,2,2,1",options="header"]
|===
|ID |Title |Kind |Direction |Frequency |Source |Destination |Protocol

|<<REF_IDX-FLOW_FLOW_COFFEE_OTA_ROLLOUT,FLOW-COFFEE-OTA-ROLLOUT>> |<<REF_IDX-FLOW_FLOW_COFFEE_OTA_ROLLOUT,OTA Rollout Interaction Flow>> |security |outbound |scheduled |<<REF_IDX-CATALOG_ACT_FLEET_OPERATOR,Fleet Operator>> |<<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_OTA_UPDATE_AGENT,OTA Update Agent>> |mqtt

== Traceability Appendix

=== Requirement Details
[[REF_REQ_REQ_COF_001]]
==== REQ-COF-001

While <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_STATE_FLEET_OPERATION_ACTIVE,coffee machine fleet operation is active>>, when <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_EVT_BREW_CYCLE_COMPLETED,brew cycle completed event is received>>, <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_THE_COFFEE_FLEET_SYSTEM,the coffee fleet system>> shall publish <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_DATA_BREW_TELEMETRY,brew telemetry>> to <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_FLEET_INGESTION_API,fleet ingestion api>> for <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_ACT_BARISTA,barista>> operations.


NOTE: Primary machine-to-cloud <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_TELEMETRY,telemetry>> contract.
